<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:palen.html>palen</a></i>. ***palisade.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a> (56352)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:palissade.html>palissade</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">palissada</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">palissa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">pal</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or possibly a from Gallo-Romance <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*pālīcea</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pālus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palisades.html>palisades</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A long, strong stake, one end of which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> set firmly in the ground, and the other sharpened.</li>
<li>A wall of wooden stakes, used as a defensive barrier.</li>
<li>A line of cliffs, especially one showing basaltic <a href = vnd.unilang:columns.html>columns</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> row of cells. e.g.: <a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a> mesophyll cells.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms CategoryTreeTag" data-ct-mode="20" data-ct-options="{quot;modequot;:20,quot;hideprefixquot;:10,quot;showcountquot;:true,quot;namespacesquot;:false,quot;notranslationsquot;:false}"><div class="CategoryTreeSection"><div class="CategoryTreeItem"><span class="CategoryTreeBullet"><span class="CategoryTreeToggle" data-ct-title="English_terms_derived_from_the_PIE_root_*peh₂ǵ-" data-ct-state="collapsed">►</span> </span> English <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> derived from the PIE root *peh₂ǵ-‎ <span title="Contains 0 subcategories, 8 pages, and 0 files" dir="ltr">(0 c, 8 e)</span></div><div class="CategoryTreeChildren" style="display:none"></div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:palisades.html>palisades</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">palisading</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">palisaded</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually in the passive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To equip with a <a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a>.</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">paillasse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">palea</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">paillasse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">pagliaccio</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">palea</i>. </p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">buffoon</span>, a <a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hansworst.html>hansworst</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pias.html>pias</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sul.html>sul</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zot.html>zot</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:palladium.html>palladium</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παλλάδιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">palládion</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">statue of <a href = vnd.unilang:pallas.html>Pallas</a> Athena</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:palladium.html>palladium</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:palladium.html>palladia</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:palladium.html>palladium</a></a>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">safeguard</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something that guarantees protection</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pandemus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πάν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pán</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δῆμος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dêmos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the people</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. ***pang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a> (12834)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The origin of the noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> uncertain;<sup id="cite_ref-OED_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-OED-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> possibly derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*pange</i>, perhaps an altered form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">prange</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">prōnge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">affliction, agony, pain; pointed instrument</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as in <i>prongys of deth</i> (“pangs of death, death throes”), from Anglo-<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pronga</i>, of unknown origin. Perhaps connected with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">prange</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pranghe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">instrument for pinching</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">prang</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse restraint; fetter, neck iron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">prange</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pole, stake; (<i>possibly</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of pillory or stocks</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-OED_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-OED-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">pyngan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to prick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The word may thus be related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">prong</i>.
</p><p>The verb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from the noun.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pangs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A paroxysm of extreme physical pain or anguish; a feeling of sudden and transitory agony; a throe.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1591</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_VI,_Part_2" class="extiw" title="w:Henry VI, Part 2">The Second Part of <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> the Sixt,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="with the Death of the Good Duke Hvmfrey">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act III, scene iii], <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=uNtBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=RA1-PA137">page 137</a>, column 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><i>War</i>[<i><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></i>]. See how the <b>pangs</b> of death do make him grin. / <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sal.html>Sal</a></i>[<i>isbury</i>]. Diſturbe him not, let him paſſe peaceably.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1601–1602</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twelfth_Night" class="extiw" title="w:Twelfth Night">Twelfe Night, or VVhat You VVill</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act III, scene iv], <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=uNtBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA269">page 269</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> knight dubb'd with vnhatche'd <a href = vnd.unilang:rapier.html>Rapier</a>, and on carpet conſideration, but he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a diuell in priuate brall, soules and <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> hath he diuorc'd three, and his incenſement at this <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ſo implacable, that ſatisfaction can be none, but by <b>pangs</b> of death and ſepulcher: Hob, nob, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> his word: giu'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> or take'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="ante">a.</abbr></i> <b>1722</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matthew_Prior" class="extiw" title="w:Matthew Prior">Matthew Prior</a>,  “Written in Lady Howe’s Ovid’s Epistles”, in  <cite>The Poetical Works of Matthew Prior, Esq.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title=" | ... |  To which is Prefixed the Life of the Author.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, Edinburgh |  Printed by Mundell and Son,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Royal Bank Close.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published 1793, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/931361946">931361946</a></small> |  republished in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Anderson_(editor_and_biographer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Anderson (editor and biographer)">Robert Anderson</a>, editor, <cite>The Works of the British <a href = vnd.unilang:poets.html>Poets</a>.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="With Prefaces, Biographical and Critical">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, volume VII, London |  Printed for John amp; Arthur Arch; and for Bell amp; Bradfute, and J. Mundell amp; Co. Edinburgh, 1795, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/221535929">221535929</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=90wwqMPHlHYCamp;pg=PA57-IA456">page 456</a>, column 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But, <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a>! what <b>pangs</b> torment the deſtin’d heart, / That <a href = vnd.unilang:feels.html>feels</a> the wound, yet dare not ſhow the dart; / What eaſe could <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ovid" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ovid">Ovid</a> to his ſorrows give, / Who muſt not ſpeak, and therefore cannot live?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1862</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christina_Rossetti" class="extiw" title="w:Christina Rossetti">Christina <a href = vnd.unilang:rossetti.html>Rossetti</a></a>,  “In the Round Tower at Jhansi, June 8, 1857”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Goblin_Market_and_Other_Poems" class="extiw" title="w:Goblin Market and Other Poems"><a href = vnd.unilang:goblin.html>Goblin</a> Market and Other Poems</a></cite>, Cambridge; London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macmillan_Publishers" class="extiw" title="w:Macmillan Publishers">Macmillan amp; Co.</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="and 23, Henrietta Street, Covent Garden. London.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/36794247">36794247</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=fbdBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PA31">page 31</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Will it hurt much?"—"No, mine own: / I wish I could bear the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> for both." / "I wish I could bear the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> alone: / Courage, dear, I am not loth."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1888</b> May,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oscar_Wilde" class="extiw" title="w:Oscar Wilde"><a href = vnd.unilang:oscar.html>Oscar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>Wilde</a></a>,  “The <a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>Nightingale</a> and the Rose”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Happy_Prince_and_Other_Tales" class="extiw" title="w:The Happy Prince and Other Tales">The Happy Prince and Other Tales</a></cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Nutt_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:David Nutt (publisher)">David Nutt</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="270 Strand.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/595167">595167</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/happyprinceother02wild/page/37/mode/1up">pages 37–38</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">So the <a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>Nightingale</a> pressed <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> against the thorn, and the thorn <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a> her heart, and a fierce <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> of pain shot through her. Bitter, bitter <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the pain, and <a href = vnd.unilang:wilder.html>wilder</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:wilder.html>wilder</a> grew her song, for she <a href = vnd.unilang:sang.html>sang</a> of the Love that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> perfected by Death, of the Love that <a href = vnd.unilang:dies.html>dies</a> not in the tomb.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sudden sharp feeling of an emotional or mental nature, as of joy or sorrow.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1843</b> December 19,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="w:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>,  “Stave Five. The End of It.”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Christmas_Carol" class="extiw" title="w:A Christmas Carol">A Christmas <a href = vnd.unilang:carol.html>Carol</a>. In Prose. Being a Ghost Story of Christmas</a></cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chapman_%26_Hall" class="extiw" title="w:Chapman amp; Hall">Chapman amp; Hall</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="186, Strand">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/55746801">55746801</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/christmascarolin20dickpage/159/mode/1up">pages 158–159</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> not <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> far, when coming on towards him he beheld the portly gentleman, who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> walked into his counting-house the day before, and <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>, "Scrooge and Marley's, I believe?"  It sent a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> across his heart to think how this old gentleman would look upon him when they <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a>; but he <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> what path lay straight before him, and he <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> it.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1867</b> February,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oliver_Wendell_Holmes_Sr." class="extiw" title="w:Oliver Wendell Holmes Sr.">[<a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a> Wendell Holmes Sr.]</a>,  “The Guardian Angel”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Atlantic" class="extiw" title="w:The Atlantic">The Atlantic Monthly. A Magazine of Literature, Art, and Politics</a></cite>, volume XIX, number CXII, Boston, Mass. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ticknor_and_Fields" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ticknor and Fields">Ticknor and Fields</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="124 Tremont Street.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/612185692">612185692</a></small>, chapter VII (<a href = vnd.unilang:myrtle.html>Myrtle</a>’s Letter.—The Young <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a>’s Pursuit.), <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=IelIAAAAcAAJamp;pg=PA141">page 141</a>, column 2:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> startled with a piece of information which <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> him such an exquisite <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></b> of delight that he could hardly keep the usual quiet of his demeanor.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">pangs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">panging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">panged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cause to have great pain or suffering; to torment, to torture.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1613</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a> |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Fletcher_(playwright)" class="extiw" title="w:John Fletcher (playwright)">[John <a href = vnd.unilang:fletcher.html>Fletcher</a>]</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_VIII_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Henry VIII (play)">The Famous History of the Life of King <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> the Eight</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act II, scene iii], <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=uNtBAQAAMAAJamp;pg=RA1-PA214">page 214</a>, column 2:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Yet if that quarrell, Fortune, to diuorce / It from the bearer, '<a href = vnd.unilang:tis.html>tis</a> a ſufferance, <b>panging</b> / As ſoule and <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> ſeuering.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1919</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christopher_Morley" class="extiw" title="w:Christopher Morley">Christopher Morley</a>,  “On Unanswering Letters”, in  <cite>Mince Pie: Adventures on the Sunny Side of <a href = vnd.unilang:grub.html>Grub</a> Street</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_H._Doran_Company" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George H. Doran Company">George H. Doran Company</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/753772533">753772533</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/mincepieadventur00morl/page/40/mode/1up">page 40</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And perhaps a not altogether false little story could be written about a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> who never visited those most dear to him, because it <b>panged</b> him so to say good-bye when he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to leave.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paniek.html>paniek</a> (1630)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pansa.html>pansa</a> (68146)</h1><br></body> 
***pansy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a> (48725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">pensée</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thought</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, as the plant resembles someone that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in deep thought, with a lowered head.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pansies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A cultivated flowering plant, derived by hybridization within species <i><a href = vnd.unilang:viola.html>Viola</a> tricolor</i>.</li>
<li>A deep purple colour, like that of the <a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a> colour: <span style="background-color:604E97; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any of various nymphalid butterflies of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Junonia" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Junonia"><i>Junonia</i></a></span>. Also called arguses.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A male homosexual, especially one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> effeminate.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A timid, weak <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> or boy; a wuss.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">male homosexual</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">friend of Dorothy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">omi-palone</span>; see also Thesaurus:male homosexual</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">effeminate <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mama.html>mama</a>'s boy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sissy.html>sissy</a></span>; see also Thesaurus:effeminate <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Wimpy; spineless; feeble.</li>
<li>Of a deep purple colour, like that of the <a href = vnd.unilang:pansy.html>pansy</a>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pantoffel.html>pantoffel</a> (56346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pantoffel.html>pantoffel</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pantoeffel</i>. Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:pantoufle.html>pantoufle</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pantoffel.html>pantoffel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pantoffels.html>pantoffels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pantoffel.html>pantoffeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">slipper</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">bedroom or house slipper</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pantser.html>pantser</a> (14518)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">panser</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">pantzer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">panciere</i> (whence Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">panchier</i>), from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">panse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">panceria</i>. The current spelling and pronunciation <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:panzer.html>Panzer</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pantser.html>pantser</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pantsers.html>pantsers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pantser.html>pantsertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">armor</span> (<i>US</i>), <span class="Latn" lang="en">armour</span> (<i>UK</i>)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***pap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pap.html>pap</a> (679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pappen.html>pappe</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pap.html>pap</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pappen.html>pappen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papje.html>papje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></li>
<li>porridge</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shorter form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papa.html>papa</a></i>, usually considered more grown-up, whereas <i><a href = vnd.unilang:papa.html>papa</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered rather child-like.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_10">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pap.html>pap</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paps.html>paps</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:pa.html>Pa</a>, dad</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:papaya.html>papaya</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arawak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Arawak language">Arawak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="arw">papáia</i>

</p>

***papier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a> (1971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">papȳrus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πάπυρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pápuros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> paper (A material used for writing or printing on, made from cellulose pulp rolled into thin sheets.)</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> money (cf. <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> sense of <span class="Latn" lang="en">paper</span>)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paracetamol.html>paracetamol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:acetaminophen.html>acetaminophen</a> (white crystalline compound used in medicine as an anodyne to relieve pain and reduce fever)</li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:paracetamol.html>paracetamol</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">parade</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">parade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paard.html>paard</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paradigma.html>paradigma</a> (44879)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">paradīgma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παράδειγμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parádeigma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paradijs.html>paradijs</a> (3618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:paradijs.html>paradijs</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">paradīs</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">paradīsus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παράδεισος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parádeisos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Iranian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Iranian language">Proto-Iranian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ira-pro">*paridayjah</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
